    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[Description], [p].[DiscountPercentage], [p].[ImageUrl], [p].[IsActive], [p].[Line], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [p].[Status], [p].[StockQuantity], [p].[Style], [p].[UpdatedAt], [c].[Id] AS [Id0], [c].[CreatedAt] AS [CreatedAt0], [c].[Description] AS [Description0], [c].[ImageUrl] AS [ImageUrl0], [c].[IsActive] AS [IsActive0], [c].[Name] AS [Name0], [c].[UpdatedAt] AS [UpdatedAt0]
    FROM [Products] AS [p]
    INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c] ON [p].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
    WHERE [p].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [s]
LEFT JOIN [ProductImages] AS [p0] ON [s].[Id] = [p0].[ProductId]
ORDER BY [s].[Id], [s].[Id0]
